# Prompt suffix append: "No zoom."

## Summary

- Updated at (UTC): 2026-05-18T15:22:38.113402+00:00
- File: `dataset/annotations/samples.json`
- Fields: `prompt`, `video_generation_prompt`
- Suffix: `No zoom.`
- Total samples: **486**
- Tasks modified: **486**

## Rules

1. Already ends with `No zoom.` -> no change
2. Ends with `No zoom` (no period) -> append `.` only
3. Otherwise -> append ` No zoom.`
